<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue occurs when incorrect Siebel jar files are (Siebel.jar and SiebelJI_enu.jar) copied under&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib/&lt;/em&gt; directory.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the latest&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;files from &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES\ &lt;/em&gt;directory from the Siebel server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;FTP both the files to the &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt; directory on PowerCenter server machine by replacing the existing jar files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the session.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to install PowerExchange for Siebel on server and client component:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run &lt;em&gt;install.bat&lt;/em&gt; from the installation package.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the &lt;em&gt;Informatica installation&lt;/em&gt; directory.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;By default, the server components are installed in the following location:&lt;em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;C:\Informatica\&amp;lt;version folder&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Install&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;to begin the installation.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Done&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;when the installation is complete.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;To verify if the installation is successful, verify if the following files are copied to the specified location:&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;lt;Powercenter installation directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;pmsiebeleimloaderct.dll&lt;br /&gt;pmsiebeleimreaderct.dll&lt;br /&gt;pmsiebeleimvldn.dll&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_EN.res&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_PT_BR.res&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;lt;Powercenter installation directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/javalib&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;FieldName.properties&lt;br /&gt;pmSiebel.jar&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&amp;lt;Powercenter installation directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;To install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component on the UNIX platforms that use the command line interface, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter&lt;em&gt; sh install.sh&lt;/em&gt; (./install.sh) at the prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the path to the Informatica installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;By default, the server components are installed in the following location:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;User Home Directory&amp;gt;/Informatica/&amp;lt;version folder&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div class=&quot;Task&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;To verify if the installation is successful, verify if the following files are copied to the specified location:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimloaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimreaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_EN.res&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_PT_BR.res&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;FieldName.properties&lt;br /&gt;pmSiebel.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/Plugin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;If the files are not copied, copy them manually.&lt;/div&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Register Plug-in&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;A plug-in is an XML file that defines the functionality of PowerExchange for Siebel.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to register plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 1: GUI&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the Plug-Ins.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to &lt;em&gt;Actions &amp;gt; Register Plug-in&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; file. If you are not launching the administrator console from Informatica server machine, copy the file&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;from server machine to the client machine where you are launching Administrator console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 2: Command line&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, launch command prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the below command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For details on registerplugin command, refer &lt;em&gt;Command Reference &amp;gt; pmrep Command Reference&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Do you want to proceed to configure the Java Properties for IS?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;To install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component on the UNIX platforms that use the command line interface, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter&lt;em&gt; sh install.sh&lt;/em&gt; (./install.sh) at the prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the path to the Informatica installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;By default, the server components are installed in the following location:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;User Home Directory&amp;gt;/Informatica/&amp;lt;version folder&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div class=&quot;Task&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;To verify if the installation is successful, verify if the following files are copied to the specified location:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimloaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimreaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_EN.res&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_PT_BR.res&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;FieldName.properties&lt;br /&gt;pmSiebel.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/Plugin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;If the files are not copied, copy them manually.&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#12345400-9d72-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e0910f20-a2ed-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back12345400-9d72-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#e0910f20-a2ed-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;GUID-D6590803-73BF-405E-BDFA-A09676D17959__GUID-6102C8F6-46BA-41EB-9A14-5AFF42C97E2D&quot; class=&quot;section&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component on the UNIX platforms that use the command line interface, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter&lt;em&gt; sh install.sh&lt;/em&gt; (./install.sh) at the prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the path to the Informatica installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backe0910f20-a2ed-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e0910f20-a2ed-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c5d51850-9746-11e5-8526-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e0910f20-a2ed-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;727bd7d0-9dad-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Configure Java Properties&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Steps to configure Java properties for PowerCenter Integration Service process that runs Siebel sessions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Launch the Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Integration Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Processes tab.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://c01f6126210a5be0f8c1-712487a4d7ba57ee5997b6d7146a9d67.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/siebel_java-1450168800861.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following table describes the properties you configure:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Classpath&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;You can   set the CLASSPATH to any JAR files that you need to run a session that   requires java components. The PowerCenter Integration Service appends the   values you set to the system CLASSPATH.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Minimum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Minimum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 32 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 70M for 70 MB.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Maximum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Maximum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 64 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 90M for 90 MB.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To copy the Siebel API libraries:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;and &lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; files in the following directory:&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the PowerCenter Client machine:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\client\bin\javalib&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the PowerCenter Services machine:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#cb454ad0-a308-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#e5b7d980-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backcb454ad0-a308-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#e5b7d980-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs when Siebel API libraries from the machine where Siebel is installed are not copied to the PowerCenter Client Machine and to the machine where the repository&amp;nbsp;service and Integration Service processes are running.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;when the&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Server component is not installed in the PowerCenter server.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;has&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;server, client and repository component, if the server component is not installed then the sessions will fail with this error.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;JSDK_42001&amp;nbsp;[ERROR] Cannot get object class for : com/informatica/powerconnect/siebel/server/writer/SiebelWrtPlugin.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762&amp;nbsp;[ERROR] java.lang.NoClassDefFoundError: com/informatica/powerconnect/siebel/server/writer/SiebelWrtPlugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762&amp;nbsp;[ERROR] Caused by: java.lang.ClassNotFoundException: com.informatica.powerconnect.siebel.server.writer.SiebelWrtPlugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;when the&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Server component is not installed in the PowerCenter server.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;has&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;server, client and repository component, if the server component is not installed then the sessions will fail with this error.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;server component in the Informatica server machine(s).&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Steps to configure Java properties for PowerCenter Integration Service process that runs Siebel sessions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Launch the Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Integration Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Processes tab.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://c01f6126210a5be0f8c1-712487a4d7ba57ee5997b6d7146a9d67.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/siebel_java-1450168800861.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following table describes the properties you configure:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Classpath&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;You can   set the CLASSPATH to any JAR files that you need to run a session that   requires java components. The PowerCenter Integration Service appends the   values you set to the system CLASSPATH.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Minimum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Minimum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 32 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 70M for 70 MB.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Maximum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Maximum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 64 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 90M for 90 MB.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Install&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#1805c230-a306-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b0184200-9d5c-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back1805c230-a306-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#b0184200-9d5c-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;A plug-in is an XML file that defines the functionality of PowerExchange for Siebel.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to register plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 1: GUI&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the Plug-Ins.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to &lt;em&gt;Actions &amp;gt; Register Plug-in&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; file. If you are not launching the administrator console from Informatica server machine, copy the file&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;from server machine to the client machine where you are launching Administrator console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 2: Command line&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, launch command prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the below command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is&lt;em&gt; pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer &lt;em&gt;copies pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to &lt;em&gt;Exclusive.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 1: GUI&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 2: Command line&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i $INFA_HOME/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back46a82400-a3e9-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#46a82400-a3e9-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#78bcf2a0-9dad-11e5-850c-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#fcbb2600-9dab-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back78bcf2a0-9dad-11e5-850c-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#fcbb2600-9dab-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Steps to configure Java properties for PowerCenter Integration Service process that runs Siebel sessions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Launch the Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Integration Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Processes tab.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://c01f6126210a5be0f8c1-712487a4d7ba57ee5997b6d7146a9d67.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/siebel_java-1450168800861.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following table describes the properties you configure:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Classpath&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;You can   set the CLASSPATH to any JAR files that you need to run a session that   requires java components. The PowerCenter Integration Service appends the   values you set to the system CLASSPATH.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Minimum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Minimum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 32 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 70M for 70 MB.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Maximum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Maximum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 64 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 90M for 90 MB.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/table&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backfcbb2600-9dab-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#fcbb2600-9dab-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c5d51850-9746-11e5-8526-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#fcbb2600-9dab-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;b4290b80-9dad-11e5-9198-bc764e10c19d&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Copying Siebel API Libraries&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Copy the Siebel API libraries from the machine where Siebel is installed to the PowerCenter Client machine and the machines where the PowerCenter Integration Service process runs.&lt;strong&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; files in the following directory:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the PowerCenter Client machine:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\clients\PowerCenterClient\client\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the machine that run the PowerCenter Integration Service process:&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Installation is Complete&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following errors is logged into the session log when running a PowerCenter session connecting to Siebel target using&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;SiebelWrt_1048 : [ERROR] Btree driver failed in restoreData.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] com.informatica.powercenter.sdk.SDKException&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR]&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;at com.informatica.powerconn&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This error occurs when the generated primary key (GPK) field of the Siebel&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;target is not linked to another transformation. When the GPK field of the target&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;is not linked, then the BTree creation fails.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, connect the GPK field for the parent Business Component to another transformation in the mapping.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7f1590f0-a3eb-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5856c7e0-a26f-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7f1590f0-a3eb-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#5856c7e0-a26f-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following errors is logged into the session log when running a PowerCenter session connecting to Siebel target using&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;SiebelWrt_1048 : [ERROR] Btree driver failed in restoreData.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] com.informatica.powercenter.sdk.SDKException&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR]&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;at com.informatica.powerconn&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This error occurs when the generated primary key (GPK) field of the Siebel&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;target is not linked to another transformation. When the GPK field of the target&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;is not linked, then the BTree creation fails.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, connect the GPK field for the parent Business Component to another transformation in the mapping.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back5856c7e0-a26f-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5856c7e0-a26f-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#c5d51850-9746-11e5-8526-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5856c7e0-a26f-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;7abe8ad0-9db4-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Designer Issues&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following Designer issues occur while importing the Siebel Objects:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue occurs if the Java SDK Minimum Memory is set to a lower value.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;Solution&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue occurs when incorrect Siebel jar files are (Siebel.jar and SiebelJI_enu.jar) copied under&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib/&lt;/em&gt; directory.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the latest&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;files from &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES\ &lt;/em&gt;directory from the Siebel server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;FTP both the files to the &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt; directory on PowerCenter server machine by replacing the existing jar files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the session.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;2014-04-01 13:43:18 : ERROR : (10718 | READER_1_1_1) : (IS | Integration_Service) : node02 : SDKS_38200 : Partition-level [AMGDSQ_USCIS_EB5_Investment]: Plug-in #401901 failed in init().&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue occurs when incorrect Siebel jar files are (Siebel.jar and SiebelJI_enu.jar) copied under&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib/&lt;/em&gt; directory.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, do the following:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the latest&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;files from &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES\ &lt;/em&gt;directory from the Siebel server.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;FTP both the files to the &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt; directory on PowerCenter server machine by replacing the existing jar files.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Restart the session.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to install PowerExchange for Siebel on server and client component:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to upgrade the PowerExchange for Siebel plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, go to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the below command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml -e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;PowerCenter Designer crashes without any error when selecting &quot;Import Siebel Business Components&quot;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs when the older versions of PowerCenter Client libraries are present at the beginning of the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, remove the previous versions of PowerCenter client libraries from the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine and restart the PowerCenter Designer.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To register the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;plug-in using &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;Server component. When you install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;(server component), the installer copies pmsiebel.xml&amp;nbsp;to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from Normal to Exclusive.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Navigate to &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt; on the PowerCenter server machine where repository service is running and run the following command to connect to repository:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep connect -r &amp;lt;repositoryname&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;domain_name&amp;gt; -n &amp;lt;Repository_user_name&amp;gt; -x &amp;lt;Repository_password&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following&lt;em&gt; pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command for registering&amp;nbsp;Siebel plugin:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin &amp;ndash;i &amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml &amp;ndash;e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from &lt;em&gt;Exclusive &lt;/em&gt;to &lt;em&gt;Normal&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Is the issue resolved?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;A plug-in is an XML file that defines the functionality of PowerExchange for Siebel.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to upgrade the PowerExchange for Siebel plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, go to&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml -e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For details on registerplugin command, refer&lt;em&gt; Command Reference &amp;gt; pmrep Command Reference&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] &amp;lt;com.siebel.common.common.r&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt; &amp;lt;Error&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ErrorCode&amp;gt;8211&amp;lt;/ErrorCode&amp;gt; &amp;lt;ErrMsg&amp;gt;Code Page &quot;ISO646-US&quot; is not supported. Use &quot;-encoding&quot; option to change the file encoding. (SBL-JCA-328) &amp;lt;/ErrMsg&amp;gt;&amp;lt;/Error&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;This error occurs when the language environment settings are not specified.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, set the language to ISO-8859-1 or any codepage that is supported by Siebel.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Example&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;For US English Language settings set the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;LANG=en_US.ISO8859-1&lt;br /&gt; LC_ALL=en_US.ISO8859-1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#336f5570-a3e9-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#bb619390-a26c-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back336f5570-a3e9-11e5-bf65-bc764e11d2f4').attr('href', '#bb619390-a26c-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;When running a PowerCenter session with a&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;connection the following error occurs:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] &amp;lt;com.siebel.common.common.r&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt; &amp;lt;Error&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ErrorCode&amp;gt;8211&amp;lt;/ErrorCode&amp;gt; &amp;lt;ErrMsg&amp;gt;Code Page &quot;ISO646-US&quot; is not supported. <div>&lt;p&gt;The following table describes the properties you configure:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Classpath&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;You can   set the CLASSPATH to any JAR files that you need to run a session that   requires java components. The PowerCenter Integration Service appends the   values you set to the system CLASSPATH.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Minimum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Minimum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 32 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 70M for 70 MB.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Maximum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Maximum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 64 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 90M for 90 MB.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Installation Steps UNIX&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;GUID-D6590803-73BF-405E-BDFA-A09676D17959__GUID-6102C8F6-46BA-41EB-9A14-5AFF42C97E2D&quot; class=&quot;section&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component on the UNIX platforms that use the command line interface, perform the following steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter&lt;em&gt; sh install.sh&lt;/em&gt; (./install.sh) at the prompt.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enter the path to the Informatica installation directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;By default, the server components are installed in the following location:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;User Home Directory&amp;gt;/Informatica/&amp;lt;version folder&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div class=&quot;Task&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;&lt;span&gt;To verify if the installation is successful, verify if the following files are copied to the specified location:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimloaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;libpmsiebeleimreaderct.so&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_EN.res&lt;br /&gt;siebeleim_PT_BR.res&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;FieldName.properties&lt;br /&gt;pmSiebel.jar&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/Plugin&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div&gt;If the files are not copied, copy them manually.&lt;/div&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This error occurs when the generated primary key (GPK) field of the Siebel&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;target is not linked to another transformation. When the GPK field of the target&amp;nbsp;Business Component&amp;nbsp;is not linked, then the BTree creation fails.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs if the Siebel jar files namely &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar&lt;/em&gt; and&lt;em&gt; SiebelJI_enu.jar &lt;/em&gt;are not copied to &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin/javalib &lt;/em&gt;and the following parameter 'Java&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;SDK Classpath'&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;is not set for the&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Integration service node&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;process.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, perform the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the &lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; and &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;files from&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES &lt;/em&gt;to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Set the Java&amp;nbsp;SDK Classpath for the Integration service running the session.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;A plug-in is an XML file that defines the functionality of PowerExchange for Siebel.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is&lt;em&gt; pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer &lt;em&gt;copies pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to register plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to &lt;em&gt;Exclusive.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 1: GUI&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the Plug-In.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to &lt;em&gt;Actions &amp;gt; Register Plug-in&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Select the&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;file. If you are not launching the administrator console from Informatica server machine, copy the file&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;from server machine to the client machine where you are launching Administrator console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Method 2: Command line&amp;nbsp;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, go to &lt;em&gt;$INFA_HOME/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i $INFA_HOME/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For details on &lt;em&gt;registerplugin &lt;/em&gt;command, refer&lt;em&gt; Command Reference &amp;gt; pmrep Command Reference&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;PowerCenter Designer crashes without any error when selecting &quot;Import Siebel Business Components&quot;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#c70599f0-a337-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#89383150-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backc70599f0-a337-11e5-9f74-bc764e10d166').attr('href', '#89383150-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs when the older versions of PowerCenter Client libraries are present at the beginning of the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, remove the previous versions of PowerCenter client libraries from the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine and restart the PowerCenter Designer.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To register the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;plug-in using &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;Server component. When you install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;(server component), the installer copies pmsiebel.xml&amp;nbsp;to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from Normal to Exclusive.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Navigate to &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt; on the PowerCenter server machine where repository service is running and run the following command to connect to repository:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep connect -r &amp;lt;repositoryname&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;domain_name&amp;gt; -n &amp;lt;Repository_user_name&amp;gt; -x &amp;lt;Repository_password&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following&lt;em&gt; pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command for registering&amp;nbsp;Siebel plugin:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin &amp;ndash;i &amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml &amp;ndash;e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from &lt;em&gt;Exclusive &lt;/em&gt;to &lt;em&gt;Normal&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;ol&gt; &lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#5e0b24d0-a88a-11e5-95c0-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#89383150-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back5e0b24d0-a88a-11e5-95c0-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#89383150-9e7d-11e5-98ea-bc764e11d2f4');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs when the older versions of PowerCenter Client libraries are present at the beginning of the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, remove the previous versions of PowerCenter client libraries from the PATH variable on the PowerCenter Client machine and restart the PowerCenter Designer.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To register the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;plug-in using &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;Server component. When you install the&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;(server component), the installer copies pmsiebel.xml&amp;nbsp;to the following directory:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from Normal to Exclusive.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Navigate to &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt; on the PowerCenter server machine where repository service is running and run the following command to connect to repository:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep connect -r &amp;lt;repositoryname&amp;gt; -d &amp;lt;domain_name&amp;gt; -n &amp;lt;Repository_user_name&amp;gt; -x &amp;lt;Repository_password&amp;gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following&lt;em&gt; pmrep registerplugin&lt;/em&gt; command for registering&amp;nbsp;Siebel plugin:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin &amp;ndash;i &amp;lt;$INFA_HOME&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml &amp;ndash;e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the repository mode from &lt;em&gt;Exclusive &lt;/em&gt;to &lt;em&gt;Normal&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;reader session fails with the following error:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;JSDK_42001 : [ERROR] Cannot get object class for : com/informatica/powerconnect/siebel/server/reader/SiebelReaderPlugin.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;when the&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;Server component is not installed in the PowerCenter server.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;has&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;server, client and repository component, if the server component is not installed then the sessions will fail with this error.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;ObjMgrBusCompLog&amp;nbsp;Error&amp;nbsp;1&amp;nbsp;008a8ad2533a0050:0&amp;nbsp;2014-04-08 11:54:25&amp;nbsp;(oracon.cpp (3842)) SBL-DBC-00111: An error has occurred writing to a record.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-import the Siebel Business object to the PowerCenter repository and ensure that all the field attributes are correct.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Steps to configure Java properties for PowerCenter Integration Service process that runs Siebel sessions:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Launch the Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Integration Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the Processes tab.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://c01f6126210a5be0f8c1-712487a4d7ba57ee5997b6d7146a9d67.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/siebel_java-1450168800861.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The following table describes the properties you configure:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;table border=&quot;1&quot; cellspacing=&quot;0&quot; cellpadding=&quot;0&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Property&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Description&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/thead&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;tbody&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Classpath&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;You can   set the CLASSPATH to any JAR files that you need to run a session that   requires java components. The PowerCenter Integration Service appends the   values you set to the system CLASSPATH.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Minimum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Minimum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 32 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 70M for 70 MB.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;tr&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;30%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Java   SDK Maximum Memory&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;td width=&quot;69%&quot; valign=&quot;top&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Maximum   amount of memory the Java SDK uses during a session.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If the   session fails due to a lack of memory, you can increase this value. Default   is 64 MB. If you want to increase the value, specify the value followed by M.   For example, specify 90M for 90 MB.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/td&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/tr&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt; to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to upgrade the PowerExchange for Siebel plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, go to&lt;em&gt;&amp;nbsp;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the following command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml -e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-import the Siebel Business object to the PowerCenter repository and ensure that all the field attributes are correct.&lt;/li&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;2015-02-23 13:22:46 : ERROR : (19590 | READER_1_1_1) : (IS | PCIS_V_MYL_QA) : node01PWCQAMYL : JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] com.informatica.powercenter.sdk.SDKException&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;2015-02-23 13:22:46 : ERROR : (19590 | READER_1_1_1) : (IS | PCIS_V_MYL_QA) : node01PWCQAMYL : SDKS_38200 : Partition-level [AMGDSQ_Quote]: Plug-in #401901 failed in init().&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This session is failing while initializing the Siebel source and could happen if the Siebel source is corrupted.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To resolve this issue, perform&amp;nbsp;the following&amp;nbsp;steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Ensure that all the fields of the Siebel Business object are correctly linked to the corresponding tables in the physical layer.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-import the Siebel Business object to the PowerCenter repository and ensure that all the field attributes are correct.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;The Designer cannot find the Siebel.jar files...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;This issue occurs when Siebel API libraries from the machine where Siebel is installed are not copied to the PowerCenter Client Machine and to the machine where the repository&amp;nbsp;service and Integration Service processes are running.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Locate the &lt;em&gt;Siebel.jar &lt;/em&gt;and &lt;em&gt;SiebelJI_enu.jar&lt;/em&gt; files in the following directory:&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;Siebel Installation Directory&amp;gt;\siebsrvr\CLASSES&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the PowerCenter Client machine:&lt;br /&gt; &lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\client\bin\javalib&amp;nbsp;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the files to the following directory on the PowerCenter Services machine:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;\server\bin\javalib&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

Use &quot;-encoding&quot; option to change the file encoding&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;When running a PowerCenter session with a&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;connection the following error occurs:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;JAVA PLUGIN_1762 : [ERROR] &amp;lt;com.siebel.common.common.r&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt; &amp;lt;Error&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ErrorCode&amp;gt;8211&amp;lt;/ErrorCode&amp;gt; &amp;lt;ErrMsg&amp;gt;Code Page &quot;ISO646-US&quot; is not supported. <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;This error occurs when the language environment settings are not specified.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

Default value for the Java SDK Minimum Memory is 32 MB and can be increased up to 70 MB.&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#d34ec350-a3e9-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9fa693d0-a26c-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backd34ec350-a3e9-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d').attr('href', '#9fa693d0-a26c-11e5-a53e-bc764e10c19d');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;A&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;session fails with following error in the Integration service log:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

Too small initial heap&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;while running&amp;nbsp;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;session.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;[ERROR] The error code for Siebel exception is '7733359'&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;PowerExchange for Siebel&amp;nbsp;session is not able to extract any records from the Siebel Contact Business Object. Session log shows the below error:&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;SiebelRdr_1045 : [ERROR] The error code for Siebel exception is '7733359'.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;SiebelRdr_1031 : [ERROR] The Integration Service could not extract data from the business component [An error has occurred writing to a record.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Please continue or ask your systems administrator to check your application configuration if the problem persists.(SBL-DBC-00111)].&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Cause&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;This issue occurs if the Siebel user does not have SSE_ROLE on the Siebel database.&amp;nbsp;The Siebel Application object manager also displays the following error messages:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;ObjMgrBusCompLog&amp;nbsp;Error&amp;nbsp;1&amp;nbsp;008a8ad2533a0050:0&amp;nbsp;2014-04-08 11:54:25&amp;nbsp;(oracon.cpp (3842)) SBL-DBC-00111: An error has occurred writing to a record.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Please continue or ask your systems administrator to check your application configuration if the problem persists.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; SQLParseAndExecute&amp;nbsp;Execute&amp;nbsp;5&amp;nbsp;008a8ad2533a0050:0&amp;nbsp;2014-04-08 11:54:25&amp;nbsp;ORA-06550: line 6, column 15:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; PL/SQL: ORA-01031: insufficient privileges&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; ORA-06550: line 6, column 1:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; PL/SQL: SQL Statement ignored&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; ORA-06550: line 22, column 15:&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; PL/SQL: ORA-01031: insufficient privileges&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;em&gt; ORA-06550: line 22, column 1&lt;/em&gt;:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Solution&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;To resolve this issue, ask the Siebel administrator to grant SSE_ROLE to the Siebel user that&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;is&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span&gt;used with PowerCenter sessions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Did this information resolve your issue?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;A plug-in is an XML file that defines the functionality of PowerExchange for Siebel.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The plug-in file for PowerExchange for Siebel is &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml&lt;/em&gt;. When you install the PowerExchange for Siebel server component, the installer copies &lt;em&gt;pmsiebel.xml &lt;/em&gt;to the following directory:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Steps to upgrade the PowerExchange for Siebel plugin:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Go to Administrator Console.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Click on the repository service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change the operating mode of the repository to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;Exclusive&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;On the Informatica server machine, go to&amp;nbsp;&lt;em&gt;&amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the below command:&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;pmrep registerplugin -i &amp;lt;PowerCenter Installation Directory&amp;gt;/server/bin/Plugin/pmsiebel.xml -e&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
